- **`SchedulerGrid` render component-splits.** Risks breaking `React.memo` identity ŌåÆ re-render regressions
  (jank, not a red test) in a virtualised grid, and every `data-testid` must survive for the 20 E2E specs.
  Low mechanical benefit ŌĆö the high-value pure part (`buildSchedulerModel`) is already extracted. *Write
  first:* a row-render-count assertion.

Coverage snapshot at this decision: **91% lines / 79% branches** (439 web tests). The branch gap is the
relevant one ŌĆö the deferred risks are branch / interaction / render-identity invariants that line coverage
does not capture, which is the whole reason "tests first" (not "more coverage") gates the deferred work.

## 2026-06-08 ŌĆö Deploy / DB-move
- **Forge static-SPA deploy guide** added (`docs/deploy.md`): DigitalOcean droplet, `Static HTML` site, `/dist` web dir, deploy script (`npm ci --include=dev` guards NODE_ENV=production skipping devDeps), SPA `try_files` fallback for `createBrowserRouter`. Friends demo stays localStorage on purpose: independent per-browser sandboxes, refresh-safe ŌĆö the server's *shared* dataset would be worse for independent play.
- **DB-move action plan** added (`docs/server-migration-plan.md`): reframes the move as a *cutover + hardening* (Phases 0/1 already done), not a build. Near-term goal = friends-demo shared dataset ON the DB (daemon + `/api` proxy + build-time `VITE_FLOATY_API` flip + Basic Auth + persistent SQLite + backups), no app code. Stages BŌĆōE (concurrency/conflict UI, real auth+isolation, Postgres) are conditional/trigger-gated. Load-bearing caveats recorded there: the flag is build-time with NO localStorage fallback (server becomes a hard dependency; rollback strands server data), optimistic concurrency needs a client conflict UI not just the env flag, and `server/` is raw `node:sqlite` (no ORM) so Postgres is a rewrite.

## 2026-06-09 ŌĆö Convergence run (P1 config)

## 2026-06-09 ŌĆö Cross-repo review fixes (round 2)
- 2026-06-09 ŌĆö server CORS (F5) ŌĆö `buildApp`'s factory default changed from fail-OPEN (`opts.corsOrigin ?? '*'`) to fail-CLOSED (`?? DEFAULT_CORS`, the localhost allow-list); `DEFAULT_CORS` is now defined+exported in app.ts and IMPORTED by index.ts (was a duplicated local const) so the factory itself is safe and the entrypoint stays the single source of the override. A wildcard now requires an EXPLICIT `corsOrigin:'*'`. Rewrote the app.test "echoes '*' by default" case into: localhost reflected + evil.test gets no ACAO header by default, and '*' echoed only when explicitly passed (review-fix-2)
- 2026-06-09 ŌĆö server bind host (F4) ŌĆö `app.listen` host default changed from `0.0.0.0` to `127.0.0.1` (localhost-only), overridable via new `FLOATY_HOST` env var for deliberate LAN/deploy exposure; server/README Env section documents the localhost default + the 0.0.0.0 override (review-fix-2)
- 2026-06-09 ŌĆö server 500 leak (F6) ŌĆö `fail()` now sends a GENERIC `{ error: 'Internal server error' }` body on the 500 branch and `console.error`s the real error server-side, instead of echoing `err.message`; the specific caller-fault 400 messages (validation / FK / constraint) are kept unchanged (review-fix-2)

(localStorage-only blame, wrong in server mode where a failed remote PUT trips it) to neutral "Changes arenŌĆÖt being saved right now ŌĆö weŌĆÖll keep retrying." ## 2026-06-11 ŌĆö Dev-server white screen: loud binding, strict port
- 2026-06-11 ŌĆö dev server (white-screen root cause) ŌĆö a 5-agent investigation (full e2e 89/89 green; code audit; Chromium+WebKit load matrix on localhost/127.0.0.1/[::1]; machine forensics; cold-boot repro of `npm install && npm run dev`) proved the app has NO silent-white path once main.tsx executes (pre-hydration renders sidebar+Loading; all failures render visible recovery screens) ŌĆö the only reproduction of the reported triad (white page + empty console + 0 KB storage) is a connection-level failure: browsing an address/port the single-family-bound Vite isn't answering. Two silent-mismatch sources: Node 17+ binds `localhost` to ::1 only (fixed earlier today: `host: '127.0.0.1'`), and Vite's silent port-bump to 5174 when 5173 is squatted (this repo + floaty-schedule + delivery-diary all claim 5173). Hardened vite.config.ts with `strictPort: true` so a taken port fails loudly at startup instead of serving the wrong URL silently; added a README "Run it" section (npm install / npm run dev / open the URL Vite prints / lsof to find squatters). Verified after change: picker role-assert PASS, eslint+tsc clean, e2e smoke 6/6 (dev-hardening)
- 2026-06-11 ŌĆö index.html (JS-blocked fallback) ŌĆö the user's white screen was REPRODUCED with javaScriptEnabled:false: the real root cause on their machine is scripts being blocked for the site (content-blocker extension allowed in incognito / per-site JS setting), which yields exactly white + empty console + 0 KB storage because nothing executes. index.html now ships a static #root placeholder ("LoadingŌĆ” if this doesn't go away, JavaScript isn't runningŌĆ”") that React replaces on mount, plus a <noscript> banner ŌĆö a JS-less load is self-diagnosing instead of silent white. Verified: JS-off shows the message, JS-on renders the picker with 0 placeholder remnants, gate green, chromium e2e 85/85 (dev-hardening)
- 2026-06-11 ŌĆö docs (white-screen wrap-up) ŌĆö promoted the JS-less-fallback call to DECISIONS.md (UI & product: "A JS-less load is never silent white" ŌĆö keep the index.html placeholder when touching that file); REFERENCE.md "Launching the app" now points at the URL Vite prints, explains the strict-port startup error, and adds a step-5 troubleshooting note for the "JavaScript isn't running" placeholder (confirmed root cause of the 2026-06-11 white-screen report: browser-level JS disabled + blocker extensions allowed in incognito); README Run-it section gains the matching JS-blocked note (docs)

## 2026-06-11 ŌĆö E2E clock determinism
- 2026-06-11 ŌĆö e2e (test time-drift) ŌĆö 14 chromium specs (scheduler/allocation/features/filters/toolbar) failed once the real wall-clock passed the seed window: seed bars live 1ŌĆō9 June 2026 (Tyler over-allocated 3ŌĆō4 June) and the scheduler origin snaps to the current week's Monday with the utilisation window running forward from today, so by 2026-06-11 every seed bar + the 3ŌĆō4 June over-marker had scrolled off-screen and each spec that clicks/hovers/drags a seed bar broke. Fixed in e2e/helpers.ts: `openApp()` now calls `page.clock.setFixedTime(new Date('2026-06-03T12:00:00'))` BEFORE `goto`, freezing test "today" inside the seed window; `setFixedTime` pins Date/now only (scroll/drag/popover timers keep running). No production or shared-domain change. Verified green: chromium 85/85, db-backed 4/4, eslint clean. Promoted a one-line standing note to DECISIONS.md (Testing & process) and added the E2E counterpart to the REFERENCE.md seed-date note (e2e determinism)

- 2026-06-14 ŌĆö code-quality/defensive ŌĆö open-source hardening pass. Added **DEFENSIVE-CODING.md** (the surface-never-swallow standard: the two-tier error model, where try/catch BELONGS vs is HARMFUL, the TSDoc/why-comment bar) and promoted the rule to DECISIONS.md + CLAUDE.md. An 8-subsystem audit confirmed the code was ALREADY defensive (zero silent swallows in any data path, rich comments throughout), so this CLOSED the real gaps rather than carpet-bombing try/catch. Behavioural fixes (all SURFACE, none swallow): AllocationBar keyboard-nudge rejection now toasts (was the one silent `catch {}`); downloadTextFile now THROWS so the backup-before-delete path (DeleteCompanyDialog / StorageRecovery / ImportExport export) can BLOCK on a failed export; a localStorage.getItem access error reclassifies to LoadError('unavailable') not 'corrupt'; rowCodec.fromRow rethrows corrupt-JSON naming table.column.id; AuthProvider validates the untrusted /api/auth/me body + always-reloads signOut, LoginScreen catches pre-response network throws; server getSession 503-frames an auth-backend failure (never serves unauthenticated); index.ts parsePort + framed boot crashes; db.ts asserts a vetted table name before SQL interpolation; txn.ts preserves the original error over a failed ROLLBACK; setActiveAccount surfaces an unknown tenant id (drops to picker); capacity.ts dev-asserts finite hours (a NaN reads as "never over"); the six entity forms now catch+surface store throws like TimeOffForm. Docs layer: public-API TSDoc/@throws/preconditions across shared/, the store CRUD throw-vs-no-op contract on the interface, component headers, and guard-comments on every "don't wrap this" pure/throw path. ImportExport now surfaces parseData's SPECIFIC reason (US-DAT-04 + data.spec/ImportExport.test assertions updated to match; REFERENCE.md unaffected). - 2026-06-14 ŌĆö code-quality/defensive ŌĆö adopted the FULL-CHAIN re-throw convention (a sibling-repo lesson): when a catch re-throws, attach the caught error as `{ cause: e }` so the whole chain survives, not just a re-worded message. ESLint `preserve-caught-error` already enforces it for NATIVE errors (it flagged rowCodec in the prior round) but is silent on custom error classes and bare `catch {}`. Made `LoadError` + `ValidationError` accept `ErrorOptions` and forward the cause; passed `{ cause: e }` at the re-throws that lacked it ŌĆö LocalStorageAdapter (storage-access / JSON.parse / migrate), ServerSyncAdapter.loadAll, the validateWrite re-tag, and transfer.parseData (bound its previously-bare catch). Documented as DEFENSIVE-CODING.md ┬¦1 and promoted to to-my-siblings principle 13 (surface-never-swallow). Gate green: root 645 + server 101 + e2e 226/226 (now incl. WebKit via e2e:all) (e336b98)

- 2026-06-16 ŌĆö scheduler/feature ŌĆö **Minimise weekends** (deferred Alpha feature #5, branch `minimise-weekends`) shipped as the two reviewable commits the plan specified. **Commit 1 (mechanical, behaviour-preserving)** introduced `src/components/scheduler/columnGeometry.ts` ŌĆö one `ColumnGeometry` (prefix-summed `offsets`/`widths`, `x`/`widthOf`/`spanWidth`, the date-keyed `xForDateInGeom`/`widthForDates`, and `indexAt` = the EXACT inverse of `x()` via binary search, round-trip unit-tested) ŌĆö and threaded it through `schedulerModel` (replaced the `origin`+`dayWidth` scalars), `DateHeader` (cell/month widths), `ResourceLane` (every overlay + the shared pointerŌåÆday inverse), `AllocationBar`/`useDragResize` (day delta is now `indexAtClientX(cur) ŌłÆ indexAtClientX(start)`, each endpoint snapped to a column independently ŌĆö `snapDeltaToDays` removed), `allocationDrag.snappedBarGeometry` (preview routed through the same geom as the commit ŌåÆ no jump on release), and `SchedulerGrid` (`todayX`/`focusX`/`totalWidth`/`visibleStartDate` from geom; the zoom/resize scroll-anchor now re-anchors the left-edge DATE on a WIDTH change only ŌĆö guarded by `days === prevDays` so a Prev/Next-week PAN still advances by preserving scrollLeft). With `minimiseWeekends=false` hard-wired the geometry is byte-identical to the old `index*dayWidth` grid ŌĆö every existing test + e2e passed unchanged (e734315). **Commit 2 (the feature)** added the device-global pref (`floaty/minimiseWeekends`, default **ON**, own key, NOT on the account / not in export ŌĆö `displayPrefs` + store `setMinimiseWeekends` + Settings ŌåÆ **Schedule** ToggleRow), the rem-based `WEEKEND_COLUMN_REM` (resolved against the root font size measured on the ResizeObserver tick; `buildColumnGeometry` caps it at `dayWidth` and only narrows at/above `DAY_COLUMN_MIN_WIDTH`), and the DateHeader "S" weekend label (both Sat+Sun, date number kept). Weekends are NOT removed ŌĆö weekend work + spanning bars still render across the narrow columns. Highest-risk traps avoided per plan: same-geom previewŌåöcommit (no release jump), exact `indexAt`Ōåö`x` inverse, and the pan-vs-zoom scroll-anchor split; `resolveDayWidth` left unchanged (the 1-week right-edge slack is cosmetic, called out so nobody "fixes" the fit and destabilises the anchor). Promoted to DECISIONS.md (UI & product ŌåÆ "Weekends minimise by default"); REFERENCE.md updated first + new US-SET-05 + `e2e/minimise-weekends.spec.ts` (4 specs: narrow+"S" default, toggle-off restores Sat/Sun, reload persistence, drag-across-weekend lands later); plan doc marked IMPLEMENTED. - 2026-06-16 ŌĆö scheduler/fix ŌĆö minimise-weekends owner-review follow-ups (two issues; the plan PREDICTED the first as a deferred follow-up, the second was a real bug). (1) **Zoom under-filled** ŌĆö a "1-week" view showed ~1.5 weeks (2w ~2.5) because `resolveDayWidth` sized columns as `avail/(weeks*7)` (7 EQUAL columns), but a minimised week occupies only `5┬ĘdayWidth + 2┬ĘweekendWidth`, leaving right-edge slack. Added a **weekend-aware fit**: `resolveDayWidth(avail, weeks, weekendWidth?)` widens the weekday columns so `weeks┬Ę(5┬ĘdayWidth + 2┬ĘweekendWidth) = avail`; SchedulerGrid passes `weekendWidth` ONLY while minimise is actually narrowing (uniform width > weekend width), else the uniform 7-column fit. Raised `MAX_DAY_WIDTH` 120ŌåÆ240 so a 1-week view can FILL a normal screen ŌĆö the 120 cap bit well before ultra-wide (the plan's "leave resolveDayWidth unchanged" note is now superseded by the owner request). (2) **Left-edge date drifted onto the weekend on every zoom flip** ŌĆö ROOT CAUSE: `weekendWidth` was fractional (`1.4 ├Ś 15.99 = 22.39`), so offsets were fractional (e.g. `offset(Jun1)=1699.12`) while the browser stores `scrollLeft` as a whole number (1699); the scroll-anchor's `geom.indexAt(1699)` then floored to the PREVIOUS (narrow Sunday) column and re-anchored a day early. FIX: **round weekendWidth to a whole pixel** (in SchedulerGrid AND defensively in `buildColumnGeometry.narrowWidth`) so every offset is an integer and the date round-trip is exact ŌĆö `dayWidth` was already integer (resolveDayWidth floors). Diagnosed with a throwaway Playwright probe (clientWidth 1320 ŌåÆ weekend 22.39, leftDate drifted `1Mon`ŌåÆ`31S`); after the fix the probe shows 1w = exactly 7 visible days with `1Mon` byte-identical across a 1wŌåÆ2wŌåÆ1w round-trip, screenshot-confirmed. Tests: `schedulerConfig.test` fit + clamp + non-finite cases; two new `minimise-weekends.spec` e2e guards (1-week fit Ōēż9 visible days; zoom-flip preserves the non-weekend left-edge date). DECISIONS.md "Weekends minimise by default" extended with the two coupled invariants (integer-pixel widths; weekend-aware fit + MAX 240). Gate green: root 675 + e2e 123. (c4f5ca2)

- 2026-06-16 ŌĆö e2e ŌĆö opt-in **Firefox/Gecko twin** of the core specs landed, mirroring the WebKit pass (06-13, 4312d7c). A `firefox` Playwright project (Desktop Firefox device, same `testIgnore` ŌåÆ the localStorage specs) made to exist by `FLOATY_FIREFOX_ONLY`/`FLOATY_FIREFOX`, run via `npm run e2e:firefox` (the *_ONLY flag both creates the project AND trims the webServer list to Vite-only ŌĆö no SQLite/auth server, no Node 24) or `npm run e2e:all` (the full three-engine matrix). Config generalised: `firefoxOnly`/`firefoxEnabled` alongside the webkit pair, and the webServer trim now keys off `viteOnly` (`FLOATY_VITE_ONLY` Ōł© `webkitOnly` Ōł© `firefoxOnly`). **Full-run ordering (owner ask):** `e2e:all` is `node scripts/e2e-all.mjs` ŌĆö TWO sequential Playwright invocations (the `FLOATY_WEBKIT` matrix = Chromium+db+auth+WebKit, THEN `FLOATY_FIREFOX_ONLY` Firefox alone), so Firefox runs second AND unconditionally (it runs even if the matrix went red; the script exits non-zero if either invocation failed, so the gate still catches it). Chose script-chaining over a `firefox` project `dependencies: ['webkit']` *precisely because* a Playwright project dependency SKIPS the dependent when the dependency fails ŌĆö which would hide a Firefox-only regression behind any red WebKit run. Also added **`npm run e2e:browsers`** (scripts/e2e-browsers.mjs): the core specs on ALL THREE engines (Chromium+WebKit, then Firefox), NO db/auth server specs ŌĆö so it's fully Vite-only via a new `FLOATY_VITE_ONLY` flag that generalises the webServer trim (renamed `altBrowserOnly`ŌåÆ`viteOnly`), letting a Chromium+WebKit core run skip the SQLite/auth servers too. `e2e:all` is the superset that adds the Chromium-only server specs; same two-invocation WebKitŌåÆFirefox shape. - 2026-06-20 ŌĆö feature/scheduler ŌĆö **Displayed utilisation % moved to the currently VISIBLE window; `overSoon` stays on the fixed 14-day window** (owner request this session). Split the old single "utilisation % / overSoon over a fixed forward 14-day window" into two signals (the per-day over-marker is a third, unchanged). Before the first scroll settles (`leftEdgeIdx===-1`) the window anchors at `ui.focusDate` (NOT `days[0]`, which is the PAST_BUFFER origin behind today) so initial numbers are sensible. A Back/Forward **pan** is handled for free: it produces a new `days` array (memo dep) while preserving scrollLeft, so `days[leftEdgeIdx]` re-resolves to the new left-edge date without `onScroll` firing. **Labels:** the header "Utilisation ┬Ę next 2w" ŌåÆ "Utilisation ┬Ę {zoom}w"; per-row + header titles ŌåÆ "over the visible N weeks"; the `overSoon` red-flag wording keeps its fixed-window phrasing. - 2026-06-20 ŌĆö feat/capacity-overage-red ŌĆö **Over-capacity day gets a CLEAR red background** (owner request this session). The per-day over-marker predicate (`capacity.ts` `dayCapacity` ŌåÆ `over: allocated > available`, STRICTLY greater; available 0 on non-working/time-off, so it also catches a zero-capacity day with any work) is UNCHANGED and stays strict ŌĆö at-capacity (8 vs 8) is NOT red. Only the RENDER strengthened: `ResourceLane.tsx` over-marker fill `bg-danger/12` (faint 12% tint, too subtle to read as red) ŌåÆ a dedicated, strongly saturated `bg-danger-cell` token (`--c-danger-cell`: light `color-mix(in oklab, var(--c-danger) 50%, white)` Ōēł rgb(251,158,161); dark `ŌĆ”60%, #0e1016` Ōēł rgb(147,73,86)), keeping the `border-t-[3px] border-danger` band as the non-colour-alone shape cue. NOTE the rationale is NOT an AA contrast pairing ŌĆö the over-marker cell is EMPTY (no text), and the allocation bars layered on top (DOM order) carry their own opaque WCAG-tuned fills, so the cell red has no text-contrast constraint and @axe-core stays green even at full saturation (the `danger-soft`/`danger-soft-ink` AA pairing applies only to the danger BUTTON, not this cell). (An earlier draft on this branch wrongly used `bg-danger-soft` ŌĆö a pale pink button tint Ōēł the old /12 blush, so the "clear red" acceptance was UNMET; superseded.) Corrected stale "zero-capacity day" wording to "allocated > available (the over / red-background signal)" in CLAUDE.md, DECISIONS.md, `schedulerModel.ts`, `capacity.ts`; SchedulerGrid sr-only "Scheduled on N zero-capacity days" ŌåÆ "Over capacity on N days". - 2026-06-22 ŌĆö code-review/remediation ŌĆö **Three write-boundary integrity fixes (owner-supplied review).** (1) **Days-mode silent clamp (High):** `AllocationModal` let "Days of work" derive an hours/day the store then silently clamped to `MAX_HOURS_PER_DAY` (24), discarding the entered volume ŌĆö the modal previewed e.g. 40h/day but saved 24. Submit now REJECTS in days mode when `effHoursPerDay > MAX_HOURS_PER_DAY` ("ŌĆ”increase Days over or reduce Days of work"), so preview === saved; same guard added to hourly mode (the field caps at 24 on blur, but an Enter-submit without blur could still carry a larger value). (2) **Duplicate built-in Internal via server (Med):** the store strips `builtin` from public client CRUD, but DIRECT API writes passed `builtin:true` straight through, so a second Internal could be minted (and `internalClientFor` is first-match ŌåÆ shadowed under an arbitrary one, invisible since the client list hides built-ins). `validateWrite` (server) now rejects a clients write that would add a SECOND builtin to an account (another builtin with a different id exists); updating the SAME builtin and one-per-account-each are still allowed. (3) **External invariants UI/import-only (Med):** external/3rd-party resources are capacity-free (no load, no time off), but the shared write boundary only checked the resource EXISTS. Enforced in the shared domain core so store + server inherit it: `assertResourceExists` rejects time-off on an external; `assertAllocationRefs` gains an optional `hoursPerDay` and rejects a non-zero load on an external (store passes it on add + a broadened update guard that now also fires on a hours-only patch; server passes `row.hoursPerDay`). Import (`remapAndValidateImport`) now DROPS external time-off (was kept) to match ŌĆö external allocation load was already coerced to 0. - 2026-06-24 ŌĆö fix/over-marker-weekends ŌĆö **The per-day over-marker no longer flags a weekend a bar merely spans** (owner reported weekends counting as over-capacity). `capacity.ts` `allocatedHoursOnDay` is now **weekend-aware**: it takes the `resource` (was `resourceId`) and skips a weekend-aware allocation's hours on the resource's non-working weekdays, via the domain's single source of truth `isWeekendAware(resource.workingDays, alloc.ignoreWeekends)` (same predicate that already governs duration/drag/utilisation, so the over-marker can't disagree with them). Net effect on the `over: allocated > available` flag: a normal allocation spanning Sat/Sun contributes 0 there ŌåÆ NOT over (the weekend keeps only the grey "unavailable" tint); a **time-off** day a working allocation covers stays over (a real conflict ŌĆö deliberately distinct from a spanned weekend, per owner); a weekend an allocation opts into via `ignoreWeekends` stays over against the MonŌĆōFri person's 0 weekend capacity (owner: weekends count *only* when included). This SUPERSEDES the "also catches a zero-capacity day with any work" wording from the 2026-06-20 feat/capacity-overage-red line ŌĆö only time-off (not weekends) is now caught for the default allocation. `utilization`/`overAllocatedInWindow`/`capacityAdvisory` were already weekend-safe (they skip/`available>0`-gate zero-capacity days), so the change is inert for them; the one production caller (`dayCapacity`) passes `resource`. Tests: capacity.test.ts ŌĆö spanned-weekend contributes 0 + not over, `ignoreWeekends` weekend IS over, time-off-day still over (replaced the old "any allocation on a zero-capacity day is over" Saturday case). Docs: CLAUDE.md + DECISIONS.md over-marker invariant reworded; US-SCH-09 + REFERENCE acceptance criteria. New e2e `weekend-overmarker.spec.ts` (drives the real app: a spanned weekend adds no over-marker, include-weekends adds 2, a time-off working day adds 1 ŌĆö closing the gap where nothing asserted a spanned weekend is NOT over) + visually verified (screenshots: weekend greyŌåÆred on opt-in, time-off day red). Gate green: root 806 tests + build; e2e 148 (chromium). (pending)

- 2026-06-24 ŌĆö shadcn/feedback ŌĆö ToastŌåÆSonner bridge fix round. The store `notice`/`setNotice` API is UNCHANGED ŌĆö AppShell's effect is the sole place that turns a `notice` into UI: info toasts `duration: 4000` (auto-dismiss), error toasts `duration: Infinity` (persist until dismissed, since an error that vanishes unread is useless). **Identity-guarded clear** fixes a real AŌåÆB stale-clear race: Sonner runs `onDismiss` on a programmatic `toast.dismiss(id)` too, so the effect-cleanup that dismisses notice A's toast (on a back-to-back AŌåÆB swap) fired A's `clear` and wiped the newer B from BOTH the store and the screen; `clear` now no-ops unless `useStore.getState().notice === thisNotice` (setNotice mints a fresh object per call, so `===` is exact), and the redundant `toastIdRef`/`if(!notice)` teardown/`=== id` guard were removed (the cleanup `toast.dismiss(id)` is the whole teardown). **Theme** `themePref === 'system' ? 'system' : themePref` ŌĆö an explicit light|dark pref is concrete, a 'system' pref delegates to Sonner (it subscribes to prefers-color-scheme itself), fixing a stale-'system' bug where an OS flip left Sonner on the old scheme (the shell doesn't re-render on that) and dropping a per-render matchMedia call. **richColors stays OFF** (its light-mode error red #e60000/pink #fff0f0 is 4.34:1, under AA) ŌĆö toasts paint on floaty's AA-validated `--color-elevated`/`--color-ink`/`--color-line`; the errorŌåÆinfo visual flattening from the migration is fixed by an ADDED danger affordance (index.css `.toast-error`: `--color-danger` left accent + 1px ring + tinted error icon over the neutral surface), AA-safe in both themes. **A11y regression accepted+documented**: Sonner 2.0.7 announces ALL toasts via a single hardcoded `<section aria-live="polite">` with no clean per-type/per-toast override, so the old assertive (`role=alert`) error announcement is now polite ŌĆö a minor accepted regression rather than a fragile per-toast role hack. - 2026-06-25 ŌĆö webkit/over-marker ŌĆö RESOLVED the WebKit-only weekend-overmarker failure from #43, and it was NOT a correctness bug. Root-caused by instrumenting both render paths on WebKit vs Chromium: the over-marker lands on the CORRECT day (2026-06-15) and the CORRECT settled pixel (2484px) on every engine ŌĆö there is no date-parse divergence (the codebase is uniformly ISO-safe via date-fns parseISO + zero-padded string compares). It was a TEST timing race: navigating Time off ŌåÆ back to Schedule REMOUNTS SchedulerGrid, whose dayWidth comes from the MEASURED container width applied one tick after first paint; WebKit lays the remounted grid out a frame later, so the spec's single non-retrying `style.left` read at line 80 caught the over-marker mid-settle (intermediate dayWidth 65px ŌåÆ 2214px) before it re-rendered to 74px ŌåÆ 2484px (the count was already right, so toHaveCount didn't gate the pixel). Fix is TEST-ONLY: wrap the position assertion in expect(async () => {...}).toPass() so it re-reads BOTH lefts from one settled snapshot (same toEqual invariant ŌĆö a real wrong-day regression still fails; Chromium/Firefox pass first try). Net: e2e:browsers now FULLY green on all 3 engines (Chromium+WebKit 292, Firefox 146). NOTE for later: the remount layout-shift (intermediateŌåÆsettled dayWidth flash) is a real, separate UX characteristic of the measure-then-compute geometry ŌĆö not fixed here. (#44)

- 2026-06-25 ŌĆö scheduler/tests ŌĆö Coverage-audit remediation for the week-snap features (#54/#55). A multi-agent audit found the navigation-snap e2e tests passed for the WRONG reason: because the "Snap to week start" pref defaults ON, the Feature-2 free-scroll idle snap MASKED the Feature-1 navigation branch (proven by mutation ŌĆö disabling only the F1 branch left the test green). De-confounded by turning the pref OFF in the "navigation re-anchors" spec so only F1 can snap (now covers zoom + Next + **Prev**, which was untested), and added the distinguishing/defensive cases the audit flagged: floor-not-nearest (nudge >┬Į week ŌåÆ floors back to the CURRENT Monday, asserted by day-number), Sunday week-start (`goToDate` + free-scroll), and preserve-exact-date on a pure resize / minimise toggle (the `snap=false` branch). Extracted the snap math to a pure `weekStartSnapTarget` (`src/components/scheduler/weekSnap.ts`, behaviour-preserving) with exhaustive unit tests, plus jsdom `SchedulerGrid` wiring tests (clientWidth mock + fake timers) for drag-freeze / debounce / convergence / timer-cleanup. Every new test mutation-checked to go red under its target regression. gate green (836 vitest); e2e 163 Chromium. (#56)
- 2026-06-25 ŌĆö scheduler/cross-browser ŌĆö `npm run e2e:browsers` surfaced a Firefox-only week-snap failure that was a LATENT correctness bug, not Firefox-specific: the floor-snap read the left-edge day via `geom.indexAt(scrollLeft)` (strict floor), but HiDPI browsers (Firefox especially) can report a fractional `scrollLeft` a sub-pixel BELOW the integer column boundary, so `indexAt` resolved to the previous day and `startOfWeekISO` of it jumped the view back a whole WEEK ŌĆö the 0.5px convergence guard can't catch a week-away target. Fixed by rounding `scrollLeft` to the nearest px before `indexAt` in BOTH snap paths (`weekStartSnapTarget` + the F1 geometry re-anchor effect); the convergence check still compares the raw `scrollLeft`. New `weekSnap` unit cases (`mondayOffset ┬▒ 0.4` ŌåÆ no-op, never the prior week, minimise on/off) are red-before / green-after. Also de-flaked two cross-engine read races (the probe sampled a mid-flight programmatic scroll under parallel load ŌĆö same class as the 06-25 webkit/over-marker remount race above) by polling the left edge to a settled fixed point before asserting (assertions unchanged in strength). gate green (842 vitest); e2e:browsers green on all 3 engines (Chromium+WebKit 314, Firefox 157). (#57)

ONE multi-stage Dockerfile (`node:24-bookworm-slim` for build+api, `nginx:alpine` for web; Node 24 required for `node:sqlite`) with two targets driving two compose services. `web` (nginx) serves the built Vite SPA and reverse-proxies `/api/*` -> the `api` service (same-origin, so CORS stays fail-closed ŌĆö `CAPACITYLENS_CORS_ORIGIN` left unset); `api` runs the Fastify daemon via `npm start -w capacitylens-server` (= `tsx server/src/index.ts`) with `CAPACITYLENS_HOST=0.0.0.0`, SQLite DB on named volume `capacitylens-db` (`CAPACITYLENS_DB=/data/capacitylens.db`) + backups on `capacitylens-backups` (`CAPACITYLENS_BACKUP_DIR=/backups`), HEALTHCHECK hitting `/api/health`. No server code change: the server stays API-only, the SPA is served by nginx (NOT `@fastify/static`). The client composes `${API_BASE}/api/...`, so `VITE_CAPACITYLENS_API` is built as the ORIGIN (default `http://localhost:8080`), NOT `/api` (which would double-prefix to `/api/api/...`) and NOT empty (which disables server mode) ŌĆö deviates from the spec's literal `/api` for that reason. New `.env.example` enumerates all 26 real runtime env vars (server `CAPACITYLENS_*`/`BETTER_AUTH_*`/`PORT`/`NODE_ENV` + client `VITE_CAPACITYLENS_*`), grouped Server/Auth/SSO/Client/Process with accurate defaults; the `CAPACITYLENS_KEY_PREFIX` constant is correctly excluded (not an env read). `.dockerignore` shrinks the context (node_modules/dist/.git/*.db/scratch). Static validation only ŌĆö Docker is not installed in the build sandbox, so `docker build`/`docker compose up` were NOT run; the live build+compose smoke is DEFERRED to P0.5.2. Validated: compose YAML parses (PyYAML in a venv ŌĆö 2 services, 2 named volumes, correct targets/ports/mounts), Dockerfile reviewed stage-by-stage (workspace symlinks `@capacitylens/shared`/`capacitylens-server` resolve against the copied `shared/src`+`server/src`; tsx+fastify present in the copied `node_modules`), `.env.example` is a 1:1 match with the code's real env reads (no missing, no fictional). gate green (850 vitest + build, dist/ produced). (feat/p0.5.1-docker)

- 2026-06-26 ŌĆö security/headers ŌĆö P0.5.3: @fastify/helmet v12 (Fastify v5 major match) registered in buildApp EARLY (before route plugins). Baseline security headers ON by default ŌĆö `X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff`, a strict minimal CSP for this JSON-only API (`default-src`/`connect-src`/`base-uri 'self'`, `frame-ancestors 'none'`, `object-src 'none'` ŌĆö no script/style allowances; SPA is nginx-served), `Referrer-Policy: no-referrer`, and `X-Frame-Options: DENY` (frameguard set to deny, not helmet's SAMEORIGIN default, for legacy browsers; modern equivalent is the CSP frame-ancestors). HSTS is the ONE header gated OFF by default behind a new `AppOptions.https` flag wired from `CAPACITYLENS_HTTPS=1` (off ŌćÆ no Strict-Transport-Security; on ŌćÆ max-age=15552000; includeSubDomains) ŌĆö HSTS over plain HTTP is harmful and this server usually runs HTTP behind a TLS proxy. New app.helmet.test.ts asserts nosniff / CSP carries frame-ancestors 'none' + connect-src 'self' / referrer-policy / X-Frame-Options DENY, and HSTS absent-by-default vs present-with-https:true. Existing app-tests unaffected (additive headers; no test asserts an exact header set). gate:server green (120 server tests), gate green (850 client). (feat/p0.5.3-helmet-headers)

Boundary: exactly 32 passes (the existing 32-char-secret test is unchanged). - 2026-06-26 ŌĆö server/access-control ŌĆö P1.5: requirePermission ŌĆö an `authorize(req, reply, accountId, action: Action): boolean` helper inside `buildApp` (server/src/app.ts), capturing `db`+`authMode`. OFF MODE = NO-OP allow-all on the FIRST line (`if (authMode === 'off') return true`) ŌĆö `resolveRole`/`can` NEVER run, `req.user` is DEMO_USER, no membership read (the #1 invariant, pinned by app.authz.test.ts OFF cases incl. cross-account ids). Auth-on: `resolveRole(db, req.user!, accountId)` ŌåÆ null (non-member) ŌåÆ 403; else `can(role, action)` false (insufficient tier) ŌåÆ 403; else true. Returns false AFTER sending the standard `{ error: 'Forbidden.' }` 403, so callers guard `if (!authorize(...)) return`. No 401/503 here ŌĆö requireUser already 401'd a session-less request / 503'd an auth-backend failure upstream, so in auth-on `req.user` is a verified session user by handler time. GATED ROUTES (each uses the accountId it ALREADY derives): `GET /api/state?accountId=` (read; REPLACED the old explicit `authMode!=='off' && resolveRole===null ŌåÆ 403` with the helper ŌĆö behaviour-equivalent, single-sourced through can()); scoped `POST /api/:entity` (write, body.accountId ŌĆö only when isScopedTable); scoped `PUT /api/:entity/:id` (write, body.accountId, before ownsRow); scoped `PATCH /api/:entity/:id` (write, merged.accountId, AFTER the 404); scoped `DELETE /api/:entity/:id` (write, ?accountId=, AFTER the 400 + ownsRow 404); `POST /api/batch` (write, PRE-SCAN before the tx ŌĆö each scoped op's accountId from op.row.accountId [PUT] / op.accountId [DELETE], so a mixed allowed+denied batch is rejected WHOLE with one 403 and NO partial write); `POST /api/import` (write, body.accountId ŌĆö closes replaceAccountSlice behind membership+write). All existing ownsRow/immutability(409)/404/400 guards kept. Cross-tenant scoped read AND write now 403 in auth-on. DEFERRED (untouched): the no-arg whole `GET /api/state` read (still open for the un-migrated auth-on client ŌåÆ P1.13); account-lifecycle writes `POST /api/accounts` + `DELETE /api/accounts/:id` (NOT gated ŌĆö a freshly-signed-up auth-on user has no membership and must create their first account; there is no `createAccount` Action; brief inline P1.5-deferral comments); manageMembers/manageInvites/purge/transferOwnership (no routes yet ŌĆö matrix-only). (feat/p1.5-require-permission)
- 2026-06-26 ŌĆö server/access-control ŌĆö P1.5 follow-up (security): account hard-delete now gated `'purge'` (admin+) in auth-on, closing a cross-tenant destruction hole on BOTH vectors. `accounts` is non-scoped (ungated for the account-lifecycle deferral), but that deferral justified only CREATE (a new auth-on user must mint their first account before any membership exists); DELETE CASCADES (FK ON DELETE CASCADE wipes ALL the account's scoped data) = total tenant destruction. Previously ANY signed-in auth-on user could (1) `DELETE /api/:entity/:id` with entity==='accounts' (fell through ungated since isScopedTable('accounts') is false), and (2) `POST /api/batch` with a `{method:'DELETE',table:'accounts',id}` op (the client's real delete-company path; the pre-scan `continue`d on non-scoped tables). Both closed via the existing `authorize` helper with action `'purge'` (admin+, per "purge = hard-delete, admin-only"; NO new Action invented ŌĆö the P1.3 matrix is fixed), resolving the caller's role against the account's OWN id. Direct route: `if (!authorize(req, reply, id, 'purge')) return` before deleteRow, in a new `else if (entity === 'accounts')` branch (scoped deletes keep their `authorize(accountId,'write')`). Batch: an accounts-DELETE branch added BEFORE the non-scoped skip ŌĆö `authorize(req, reply, op.id, 'purge')` ŌĆö so a batch containing an unauthorized accounts-DELETE is rejected WHOLE (one 403, NO partial write), same as the scoped pre-scan. `POST /api/accounts` (create) + batch PUT on accounts stay OPEN (onboarding). OFF MODE STAYS NO-OP: authorize short-circuits to allow on its first line, so the default deploy / db-backed e2e can still delete companies (unchanged). Comments updated (POST route + both delete vectors) to distinguish CREATE-open / DELETE-purge-gated, noting it's an interim gate pending P2.5/P2.6 archiveŌåÆsoft-deleteŌåÆpurge. Tests (app.authz.test.ts): non-member direct DELETE + batch accounts-DELETE ŌåÆ 403 (a1 survives via member read-back, batch left no trace); viewer & editor of a1 ŌåÆ 403 (purge is admin+); admin & owner ŌåÆ 204 (direct, account gone) + admin batch ŌåÆ 200; account-CREATE exemption (201) unchanged; OFF mode direct DELETE ŌåÆ 204 + batch ŌåÆ 200 (no-op gate). DECISIONS.md P1.5 line updated. gate:server green (176 server tests), gate green, e2e green (Chromium ŌĆö db-backed OFF persistence + auth-backed login.auth both PASS). (feat/p1.5-require-permission, amended)
- 2026-06-26 ŌĆö server/access-control ŌĆö P1.6: timeOff `note` field-redacted SERVER-SIDE in the scoped read. `readSlice(db, accountId, opts)` (server/src/db.ts) gains a REQUIRED `{ includeTimeOffNote: boolean }` (NO silent default ŌĆö every caller must decide; fail-safe). When `false`, the `note` key is DELETEd from every returned `timeOff` row on the built objects BEFORE returning (key ABSENT, not null ŌĆö matches the optional-field shape) so the note is never serialized for an Editor/Viewer; `true` returns it as stored. `TenantStore.readSlice(accountId, opts)` (server/src/tenantStore.ts) threads the option through (interface + sqliteTenantStore impl). `GET /api/state?accountId=` (app.ts): AFTER the existing `authorize(req,reply,accountId,'read')` passes, `const role = authMode==='off' ? null : resolveRole(db, req.user!, accountId); const includeTimeOffNote = authMode==='off' || (role !== null && canSeeTimeOffNote(role))` ŌåÆ `store.readSlice(accountId, { includeTimeOffNote })`. OFF = trusted-local include; auth-on owner/admin include, editor/viewer OMIT; the `role !== null` guard is belt-and-braces (resolveRole is non-null since authorize('read') already proved membership) ŌĆö fail-closed. `canSeeTimeOffNote` imported from `@capacitylens/shared/domain/access`. The NO-ARG whole `/api/state` read is left UNredacted (deferred P1.13 ŌĆö moot while it already returns everything to any authed user; one-line inline NOTE added). No read caller missed (replaceAccountSlice is a write, untouched); db.tenantStore.test.ts call-sites pass `{ includeTimeOffNote: true }`. Tests: app.authz.test.ts seeds a1 with a resource + timeOff row whose note === SENTINEL_TIMEOFF_NOTE ŌĆö owner & admin ŌåÆ note PRESENT (and sentinel in body); editor & viewer ŌåÆ note key ABSENT AND sentinel NOWHERE in the raw response body (proof of server-side redaction); OFF mode ŌåÆ note PRESENT. db.tenantStore.test.ts unit: includeTimeOffNote false strips the key (absent, not null) / true keeps it. gate:server green (183 server tests, +7), gate green (880 client + build, unchanged), e2e green (163 Chromium ŌĆö db-backed OFF reads still carry notes, auth-backed login.auth PASS). (feat/p1.6-timeoff-note-redaction)
- 2026-06-26 ŌĆö server/auth ŌĆö P1.7: native socialProviders Google/Microsoft/GitHub added to the `betterAuth({...})` config in `authFromEnv` (server/src/auth.ts) from `CAPACITYLENS_<PROVIDER>_CLIENT_ID/_SECRET` env via a new `socialProvidersFromEnv(env)` helper. Each provider is ADDITIVE + FAIL-CLOSED-ABSENT: configured ONLY when BOTH its id and secret are present (Google `{clientId,clientSecret}`; Microsoft `{clientId,clientSecret,tenantId}` with `tenantId` defaulting to 'common', overridable via `CAPACITYLENS_MICROSOFT_TENANT_ID`; GitHub `{clientId,clientSecret}`); a half-set provider (id only) is skipped, and none set ŌåÆ `socialProviders: {}` (no boot refusal). Active in password/sso modes; the OFF guarantee + mode enum (off|password|sso) + the existing `genericOAuth` ('sso') plugin are UNCHANGED ŌĆö social providers coexist with genericOAuth. Better Auth 1.6.20: `socialProviders` is keyed by provider name; `auth.options` is the exact passed config (introspectable). OPEN EMAIL SELF-REGISTRATION CLOSED BY DEFAULT (secure default, Decisions ŌĆö signup is invite-only): `emailAndPassword: { enabled: mode==='password', disableSignUp: !allowOpenSignup }` where `allowOpenSignup = env.CAPACITYLENS_ALLOW_OPEN_SIGNUP === '1'` (default false). With the flag unset, `POST /api/auth/sign-up/email` returns 400 `EMAIL_PASSWORD_SIGN_UP_DISABLED` (Better Auth's BAD_REQUEST for disableSignUp). ŌåÆ CWD-relative file. WIRING (app.ts): `AppOptions.audit?` (TSDoc: ON-by-default decided at index.ts; factory defaults `noopAuditSink()` so tests + default deploy byte-identical). NEVER pass a row/body/merged OBJECT into append ŌĆö only the typed AuditRecord with changedFields=keys (the privacy core). auditWarning via a UNIFORM `x-capacitylens-audit-warning: true` response header set ONLY on append failure, on ALL six routes (keeps entity row payloads pure + solves the 204 DELETE no-body case); batch `{ok,applied,auditWarning}` + import `{...,auditWarning}` additionally carry the flag in-body (header is the primary mechanism). (1) BETTER AUTH COOKIES PINNED (server/src/auth.ts): `authFromEnv`'s opts widened from `{trustedOrigins?}` to also accept `https?:boolean`, THREADED from index.ts (which already derives `const https = process.env.CAPACITYLENS_HTTPS === '1'` for HSTS) at the existing `authFromEnv(db, process.env, {trustedOrigins})` call ŌĆö auth.ts does NOT read CAPACITYLENS_HTTPS itself (mirrors how the HSTS flag is threaded into buildApp). The `betterAuth({...})` config gains `advanced: { useSecureCookies: opts.https ?? false, defaultCookieAttributes: { sameSite:'lax', httpOnly:true } }` and `session: { expiresIn: 60*60*24*7, updateAge: 60*60*24 }`. `useSecureCookies` TIED to a real HTTPS origin via the threaded flag (the HSTSŌåöCAPACITYLENS_HTTPS coupling idiom) ŌĆö MUST be false over plain HTTP, else the browser drops the Secure session cookie ŌåÆ endless login loop (the #1 footgun; the default deploy is HTTP behind a TLS proxy, and the e2e is HTTP so login.auth would break if this were wrong). `sameSite:'lax'` NOT 'strict' ŌĆö 'strict' drops the session cookie on the top-level OAuth redirect back from the IdP ŌåÆ broken SSO; 'lax' still sends it on that GET callback and is safe. `httpOnly:true` pinned (no JS read). `expiresIn`/`updateAge` (SECONDS) match Better Auth's own defaults (7-day absolute expiry, 1-day rolling refresh), pinned so a library default change can't silently re-tune session lifetime. (2) ENTITLEMENTS SEAM (server/src/entitlements.ts, NEW ŌĆö the control-plane swap point, mirrors tenantStore.ts's documented-swap-point style): `interface Entitlements { unlimited: true }` (minimal ŌĆö default-unlimited; NO maxResources/plan/billing fields) + `entitlementsFor(accountId: string): Entitlements` returning `{ unlimited: true }` (accountId in the signature for the future per-account lookup, `void accountId` since unused today). The activeAccountId subscription now calls `refreshActive(newId)`; a new `maybeRefreshOnFocus()` calls `refreshActive(activeId)`. CRITICAL: NO parallel re-hydrate path (a React hook can't re-seed the adapter's private lastSynced ŌåÆ would desync snapshot vs data ŌåÆ next save emits a cross-account/garbage diff) ŌĆö refresh MUST reuse refreshActive in persist.ts; the token discipline also makes a late refresh after a newer switch/refresh a no-op. Focus trigger lives in the existing `canListen` block: a new `window` 'focus' listener AND the existing `visibilitychangeŌåÆvisible` branch (tab-switch/mobile) both call the throttled `maybeRefreshOnFocus`. - 2026-06-26 ŌĆö shared/domain ŌĆö P2.2 Lifecycle state machine (PURE) ŌĆö new shared/src/domain/lifecycle.ts: the Active->Archived->Soft-deleted->Purged machine for Resource/Client/Project, a pure leaf (only import = the ISOTimestamp type), mirroring the access.ts house style (named consts, fail-closed, per-export TSDoc with PURE/INVARIANT notes). EXPORTS: type LifecycleState ('active'|'archived'|'deleted'); interface LifecycleFields ({archivedAt?,deletedAt?} ŌĆö the structural constraint, transitions are generic <T extends LifecycleFields> so archive(aResource) returns a Resource with other fields untouched); const PURGE_MIN_AGE_DAYS=30 (+ internal PURGE_MIN_AGE_MS derived, no magic numbers); lifecycleStatus(entity) (deletedAt WINS over archivedAt -> 'deleted', else archivedAt -> 'archived', else 'active'; present-check via != null so SQLite/JSON null counts as absent); affordance predicates canArchive/canUnarchive/canSoftDelete/canPurge (the access.ts can* pattern ŌĆö let a caller gate without try/catch + SINGLE-SOURCE each transition's guard); transitions archive(e,nowISO)/unarchive(e)/softDelete(e,nowISO). DESIGN CALLS (documented in a header block + TSDoc): (1) transitions are STRICT ŌĆö THROW a plain Error on an invalid source state (re-archive/double-delete/unarchive-a-tombstone) rather than silently idempotent ŌĆö matches the domain fail-loud invariant-throw idiom (assertScopedRefs/findOwned throw plain Error; NO custom error classes in shared) + DEFENSIVE-CODING 'never soften an integrity throw'; the wiring layer (P2.5) pre-checks via the exported can* predicates. (2) softDelete REFUSED unless 'archived' (delete-needs-archival, the load-bearing Decisions rule) and PRESERVES archivedAt (tombstone keeps its archive time, still reads 'deleted'). (3) unarchive clears archivedAt by DELETING the key (round-trips ABSENT = active, the P2.1 convention) and refuses a 'deleted' tombstone. (4) canPurge FAIL-CLOSED (purge is destructive): true IFF state 'deleted' AND nowISO-deletedAt >= PURGE_MIN_AGE_MS (inclusive 30d boundary); explicit Number.isNaN guard denies on missing/garbage timestamps; archival is NOT a purge precondition (an aged tombstone is purgeable regardless of how it got there). (5) PURITY: nowISO is INJECTED + parsed with Date.parse (deterministic fn of inputs); never Date.now()/argless new Date()/Math.random(). (6) NO purge(entity) fn ŌĆö purge is a server-side hard row-delete (P2.5); this module ships only the canPurge eligibility predicate. SCOPE: pure functions+consts+types ONLY; NO store/server/UI/readSlice/call-sites (P2.4 filter, P2.5 admin+purge wire it). Tests: shared/src/domain/lifecycle.test.ts (38 runtime tests) ŌĆö exhaustive 3-states x 3-transitions matrix (each transition succeeds from its one valid source, throws from the other two, with message assertions), full can* truth table, immutability (input byte-identical) + field-preservation + generic-type, canPurge boundary (exact 30d ms => true / 30d-1ms => false / 29d/31d), fail-closed (garbage deletedAt, garbage nowISO, null tombstone, future-dated negative-age), deleted-without-archivedAt => purgeable, deletedAt-wins precedence. ADVERSARIAL guard-correctness review (the can* + delete-needs-archived + purge>=30d guards are the risk surface) = VERDICT SHIP, no code defect found (9-cell matrix proven via live probe; canPurge never falls open); its only [SHOULD] was 3 missing canPurge edge tests (future-dated/deleted-without-archive/null) + the ms boundary ŌĆö ADDED via a goal-set fix subagent (test-only, lifecycle.ts unchanged). gate green (1068 client+shared tests; tsc -b/eslint/vite-build clean), gate:server green (316, Node24 ŌĆö lifecycle.ts unchanged, shared compiles into server), e2e green (168 Chromium ŌĆö inert, no call sites). - 2026-06-26 ŌĆö shared/domain ŌĆö P2.3 Resource PII obfuscation at soft-delete (PURE) ŌĆö added export obfuscateResource(resource: Resource): Resource to shared/src/domain/lifecycle.ts (the P2.2 module). Returns a NEW Resource (immutable spread+override) with `name` replaced by the deterministic token `Removed person #${shortResourceTag(id)}`; the non-exported shortResourceTag(id) strips non-alphanumerics + takes the first 4 (a UUID's leading hex), falling back to the const ANON_FALLBACK_TAG='0000' if the id is empty/has no alphanumerics (token is never a bare 'Removed person #'). SCOPE (validated): a Resource TODAY has ONLY `name` as PII (no email/SSO link ŌĆö those are MEMBER-erasure fields, P2.6); `role` is a job label ('Senior Designer'), NOT PII, so RETAINED, as are id/accountId/kind/disciplineId/employmentType/workingHoursPerDay/workingDays/projectId/color/archivedAt/deletedAt/createdAt/updatedAt. The scrub is UNCONDITIONAL across kinds: a nameless placeholder still gets the token; an `external`'s `name` (the COMPANY identifier, also PII) is erased too. PURE (token from id only ŌĆö no Date.now/Math.random), deterministic (same id->same token), immutable (input untouched). STANDALONE transform ŌĆö does NOT call softDelete; the wiring layer (P2.5 server soft-delete route) COMPOSES softDelete + obfuscateResource. [The re-review round ŌĆö below ŌĆö caught that the FIRST cut stripped unconditionally, which silently RESURRECTED an archived/soft-deleted row on any unrelated PATCH/PUT/batch edit, with no un-delete route to justify it (a HIGH regression I introduced); fixed to the pin + threaded `existing` into the PUT/PATCH/batch call sites BEFORE commit.] Safe because the dedicated lifecycle routes build rows via the pure transitions + replaceAccountSlice (never sanitizeWrite) and import uses the shared remap (not sanitizeWrite) ŌĆö both round-trip tombstones untouched; the app.test.ts full-fixture round-trip tests updated (a new stripTombstones helper), and app.lifecycle.test.ts gains BOTH forbid-SET-on-active AND preserve-on-unrelated-edit cases (PATCH/PUT/batch, resource archive + client soft-delete). validateWrite also now refuses to UN-FLAG the builtin Internal client (`builtin:false`), symmetric with the existing add-a-second guard ŌĆö a new app.lifecycle.test.ts write-guard describe locks both. - 2026-07-03 ŌĆö server/hardening ŌĆö Three pre-launch review fixes, all test-locked (server suite 391 green): (1) `Fastify({ requestTimeout: 30_000, connectionTimeout: 30_000 })` ŌĆö both defaulted to 0/disabled, leaving the direct-exposure (no-proxy) mode open to slowloris socket exhaustion; asserted via `app.server.requestTimeout`/`timeout` (Fastify 5.8.5's initialConfig typings omit requestTimeout). (2) Null/absent JSON body on generic POST `/api/:entity` + PATCH `/api/:entity/:id` returned a misclassified 500 (pre-try `body.accountId!` deref / `accountFieldsFrozen`'s `field in incoming` TypeError); both now guard `!req.body || typeof req.body !== 'object'` ŌåÆ 400 `{ error: 'A request body is required.' }`, matching the /api/batch + /api/import house pattern (PUT already guarded via `body?.id !== id`; all other body routes already used `req.body ?? {}`). Verified live via curl: 4 routes ├Ś no-body/JSON-null ŌåÆ 400. (3) The default-ON audit JSONL grew unbounded (disk-full then 500s SQLite writes): `fileAuditSink` now rotates at `maxBytes` ŌĆö rename to `<file>.1` (POSIX rename replaces the prior generation) ŌĆö bounding disk at ~2├Ś the cap; new env `CAPACITYLENS_AUDIT_MAX_MB` (positive int, default 64, fail-soft parse mirroring backup.ts's `positive` ŌĆö this bounds a log, it's not a security gate), stat/rename failures degrade via the existing latch, never throw into the request path. - 2026-07-04 ŌĆö product/multi-tenancy ŌĆö **Single company per instance by default** (owner decision after the launch review; promoted to DECISIONS.md ŌĆ║ Architecture). The multi-tenant schema/scoping stays untouched; the change is a create-time policy: new `AppOptions.multiAccount` / env `CAPACITYLENS_MULTI_ACCOUNT` (default off) ŌĆö once one `accounts` row exists, EVERY HTTP create vector (generic POST /api/accounts, PUT/batch-PUT with a fresh id, POST /api/orgs) 403s with the actionable 'This instance allows a single company. Set CAPACITYLENS_MULTI_ACCOUNT=1 to allow more.', in EVERY auth mode (deployment-shape policy, NOT authz ŌĆö no off-mode bypass, and the bootstrap token does NOT bypass it either: MULTI_ACCOUNT decides WHETHER, token/owner/admin decide WHO). One shared predicate (`accountCreateCapped`) so the rule can't drift between vectors; /api/import and /api/test/reset are documented exempt (the former can't create an accounts row, the latter is the raw production-forbidden fixture path). Rationale trail: the "open onboarding create" concern from the access-control review shrinks to a first-run bootstrap by default, and cross-tenant blast-radius findings become structurally moot on default deploys. **Boot seed became opt-in** (`CAPACITYLENS_SEED_DEMO=1`, default off ŌĆö the seed ships TWO companies, contradicting the cap): a fresh real server starts EMPTY at the create-your-company picker; the localStorage demo build still self-seeds client-side (main.tsx passes seedIfEmpty only when isDemoMode()); `scripts/dev-fullstack.mjs` sets BOTH flags so `npm run dev` stays batteries-included; `start:auth-e2e` gains MULTI_ACCOUNT=1 (its four specs provision orgs live via /api/orgs); start:e2e (db-backed) deliberately stays capped as default-policy coverage. **Client:** /api/auth/me now reports `multiAccount` + `canCreateAccount` (recomputed per request); AuthProvider/authContext carry them FAIL-OPEN (default true on demo build / fetch failure / older server ŌĆö the server is the enforcer, the client only hides the affordance); AccountPicker hides "New company" (new testid `new-company-button`) at the cap ŌĆö zero-account first-run always shows it. docker-compose forwards both new vars. Tests: server 411 (new app.singleCompanyCap.test.ts, 14; authz create-stays-open split into bootstrap/capped/multiAccount; orgs matrix threaded multiAccount:true + 4 new default-cap denials), root 1164 (AccountPicker gating incl fail-open regression guard, AuthProvider field parsing), e2e 175 incl two new db-backed cap specs (hidden button + exact 403). VERIFY (live): fresh default boot ŌåÆ [] accounts, create #1 201 ŌåÆ canCreateAccount flips false ŌåÆ #2 403 (POST and PUT-upsert), PATCH existing 200; same DB + MULTI_ACCOUNT=1 ŌåÆ #2 201; SEED_DEMO=1 fresh ŌåÆ the 2 seeded companies; screenshots of the capped picker (no button) + first-run empty state (button present). REFERENCE.md updated first; NEEDS-INPUT tripwire amended (auto-seed half RESOLVED, fake-sign-in half remains); the auth-on UI-creates-via-batch-without-membership gap stays parked Stage-C.
